> CheckImpBin <- function(db, x, type = "train",
+                         dt.dir = "~/rds/profid/analyses/profid-model/data/lodo") {
+   ## Data with missing values
+   dt <- fread(sprintf("%s/%s-%s.csv", dt.dir, db, type))
+   if (!(x %in% colnames(dt))) {
+     cat("\n", x, " has been dropped from LODO.\n\n")
+     return(invisible(1))
+   }
+   cat("\n\nCounts:\n\n")
+   print(dt[, .N, keyby = x])
+   ## Imputed data
+   dt.imp <- fread(sprintf("%s/%s-%s-imputed.csv", dt.dir, db, type))
+   if (anyNA(dt[[x]])) {
+     cat("\nSummary of values after excluding 0s and 1s:\n\n")
+     print(summary(dt.imp[!(get(x) %in% 0:1), get(x)]))
+     cat("\n")
+   } else {
+     cat("\nNo imputed values.\n\n")
+   }
+ }
>
